The_DT King_NNP Institute_NNP is_VBZ the_DT premier_JJ laboratory_NN for_IN the_DT Presidency_NNP of_IN Madras_NNP ,_, and_CC the_DT whole_NN of_IN Southern_NNP India_NNP relies_VBZ upon_IN it_PRP for_IN bacteriological_JJ and_CC serological_JJ diagnostic_JJ work_NN ,_, the_DT manufacture_NN and_CC supply_NN of_IN vaccine_NN lymph_NN ,_, prophylactic_JJ and_CC curative_JJ vaccines_NNS and_CC sera_NN ,_, and_CC for_IN expert_JJ advice_NN in_IN connexion_NN with_IN infectious_JJ and_CC epidemic_JJ diseases_NNS ._.

There_EX are_VBP yet_RB other_JJ insects_NNS ,_, which_WDT simply_RB inject_VBP the_DT virus_NN through_IN their_PRP$ bites_NNS ,_, e.g._NN ,_, the_DT rat-flea_NN ,_, conveying_VBG plague_NN from_IN an_DT infected_JJ rat_NN ,_, or_CC the_DT louse_NN spreading_VBG relapsing_VBG fever_NN from_IN infected_VBN human_JJ beings_NNS to_TO the_DT healthy_JJ ._.

The_DT hook-worm_NN ,_, for_IN example_NN ,_, which_WDT is_VBZ prevalent_NN on_IN a_DT very_RB large_JJ scale_NN in_IN this_DT Presidency_NNP ,_, causes_VBZ a_DT disease_NN which_WDT under_IN certain_JJ conditions_NNS in_IN some_DT countries_NNS ,_, has_VBZ ``_`` veritably_RB overwhelmed_VBD the_DT birth_NN rate_NN and_CC threatened_VBD the_DT very_RB existence_NN of_IN the_DT race_NN ._. ''_''
Other_JJ worms_NNS infest_VBP other_JJ parts_NNS of_IN the_DT human_JJ body_NN ._.
Thus_RB elephantiasis_NN which_WDT is_VBZ also_RB extremely_RB common_JJ in_IN some_DT parts_NNS of_IN the_DT Presidency_NNP ,_, is_VBZ a_DT chronic_JJ disease_NN caused_VBN by_IN a_DT worm_NN injected_VBN through_IN the_DT bite_NN of_IN the_DT culex_JJ mosquito_NN ;_: while_IN the_DT Guinea-worm_NNP disease_NN in_IN which_WDT the_DT infection_NN takes_VBZ place_NN through_IN drinking_NN water_NN containing_VBG infected_VBN cyclops_NNS (_( a_DT kind_NN of_IN water-flea_NN )_) ,_, has_VBZ been_VBN known_VBN to_TO cause_VB such_JJ grave_JJ inflammatory_NN swellings_NNS and_CC abscesses_NNS as_IN to_TO incapacitate_VB the_DT inhabitants_NNS of_IN villages_NNS in_IN the_DT infected_JJ areas_NNS ,_, and_CC seriously_RB hamper_JJR all_DT agricultural_JJ operations_NNS ._.

REPORT_NNP OF_NNP MR._NNP HERBERT_NNP HAWLEY_NNP ,_, M.SC._NNP ,_, F.I.C._NNP ,_, PUBLIC_NNP ANALYST_NNP WITH_NNP THE_NNP GOVERNMENT_NNP OF_NNP MADRAS_NNP ,_, ON_NNP FOOD_NNP STANDARDS_NNP UNDER_NNP THE_NNP MADRAS_NNP PREVENTION_NNP OF_NNP ADULTERATION_NNP ACT_NNP ,_, 1918_CD ._.
General_NNP ._.
On_IN my_PRP$ arrival_NN in_IN Madras_NNP in_IN January_NNP 1924_CD ,_, I_PRP was_VBD instructed_VBN by_IN the_DT Surgeon-General_JJ that_IN I_PRP was_VBD to_TO work_VB at_IN the_DT King_NNP Institute_NNP ,_, Guindy_NNP ,_, and_CC that_IN my_PRP$ first_JJ task_NN would_MD be_VB the_DT carrying_VBG out_IN of_IN such_JJ work_NN as_IN I_PRP might_MD consider_VB necessary_JJ ,_, to_TO enable_VB me_PRP to_TO recommend_VB food_NN standards_NNS for_IN adoption_NN under_IN the_DT Madras_NNP Prevention_NNP of_IN Adulteration_NNP Act_NNP ,_, 1918_CD ,_, more_RBR especially_RB standards_NNS for_IN milk_NN and_CC milk-products_NNS ._.
I_PRP found_VBD that_IN the_DT King_NNP Institute_NNP was_VBD not_RB equipped_VBN for_IN food-analysis_NN ,_, and_CC that_IN with_IN the_DT apparatus_NN and_CC chemicals_NNS in_IN stock_NN very_RB little_JJ could_MD be_VB done_VBN ._.

The_DT literature_NN on_IN the_DT subject_NN is_VBZ very_RB scanty_JJ ._.
A_DT considerable_JJ number_NN of_IN analyses_NNS of_IN buffalo_NN milk_NN are_VBP available_JJ ,_, and_CC a_DT much_RB smaller_JJR number_NN of_IN analyses_NNS of_IN cow_NN milk_NN ._.

It_PRP appeared_VBD that_IN a_DT considerable_JJ number_NN of_IN samples_NNS of_IN cow_NN milk_NN would_MD have_VB to_TO be_VB examined_VBN ,_, both_DT during_IN the_DT monsoon_NN and_CC at_IN other_JJ seasons_NNS ,_, and_CC that_IN butter_NN and_CC butter-fat_NN in_IN Madras_NNP would_MD need_VB to_TO be_VB thoroughly_RB investigated_VBN ._.
This_DT has_VBZ been_VBN done_VBN ,_, and_CC I_PRP am_VBP now_RB in_IN a_DT position_NN to_TO recommend_VB a_DT series_NN of_IN standards_NNS for_IN milk_NN and_CC milk-products_NNS for_IN official_JJ adoption_NN under_IN the_DT Act_NNP ._.

No_DT ._.
640_CD ,_, P.H._NNP ,_, dated_VBD 20th_CD March_NNP 1928_CD ._.

NOTE.42_NNP SUPPLEMENT_NNP TO_NNP THE_NNP ANNUAL_NNP REPORT_NNP OF_IN THE_NNP The_DT sewage_NN dealt_NN with_IN is_VBZ mainly_RB domestic_JJ and_CC varies_NNS in_IN quantity_NN as_RB well_RB as_IN in_IN character_NN day_NN by_IN day_NN ._.
The_DT capacity_NN of_IN each_DT of_IN the_DT open_JJ and_CC closed_VBD septic_JJ tanks_NNS is_VBZ 12,000_CD gallons_NNS ._.
The_DT tanks_NNS are_VBP built_VBN above_IN ground_NN level_NN and_CC sewage_NN is_VBZ pumped_VBN up_RP into_IN the_DT tanks_NNS ._.
Experiments_NNS were_VBD confined_VBN to_TO the_DT open_JJ and_CC closed_VBD septic_JJ tanks_NNS effluents_NNS because_IN there_EX was_VBD not_RB enough_JJ sewage_NN to_TO work_VB the_DT Imhoff_NNP tank_NN regularly_RB ,_, so_RB although_IN a_DT few_JJ analyses_NNS of_IN its_PRP$ effluent_NN were_VBD made_VBN ,_, no_DT conclusions_NNS can_MD be_VB drawn_VBN as_IN to_TO its_PRP$ functioning_NN ._.

samples_NNS were_VBD taken_VBN from_IN these_DT sources_NNS at_IN the_DT same_JJ time_NN ._.
There_EX were_VBD three_CD periods_NNS of_IN working_VBG of_IN the_DT tanks_NNS ._.
During_IN the_DT first_JJ period_NN (_( July_NNP to_TO October_NNP 1926_CD )_) the_DT volume_NN of_IN sewage_NN treated_VBN was_VBD 6,000_CD gallons_NNS per_IN day_NN and_CC this_DT gave_VBD a_DT detention_NN period_NN of_IN 24_CD hours_NNS in_IN the_DT tanks_NNS ._.
During_IN the_DT second_JJ period_NN (_( October_NNP to_TO December_NNP 1926_CD )_) the_DT flow_NN was_VBD increased_VBN ,_, consequently_RB the_DT period_NN of_IN detention_NN was_VBD reduced_VBN to_TO 18_CD hours_NNS ._.
Finally_RB from_IN December_NNP 1926_CD to_TO March_NNP 1927_CD ,_, the_DT tanks_NNS were_VBD treating_VBG the_DT full_JJ flow_NN namely_RB 24,000_CD gallons_NNS per_IN day_NN so_IN that_IN the_DT period_NN of_IN stay_NN of_IN sewage_NN in_IN the_DT tanks_NNS was_VBD only_RB 12_CD hours_NNS ._.
Period_NNP IKING_NNP INSTITUTE_NNP ,_, GUINDY_NNP ,_, FOR_NNP 1927-28_CD 43_CD difference_NN between_IN the_DT effluents_NNS from_IN the_DT open_JJ and_CC closed_VBD septic_JJ tanks_NNS ._.
